	<script>
    function getParameterByName(name) {
        name = name.replace(/[\[]/, "\\[").replace(/[\]]/, "\\]");
        var regex = new RegExp("[\\?&]" + name + "=([^&#]*)");
        var results = regex.exec(decodeURIComponent(location.search));
        return results === null ? "" : decodeURIComponent(results[1].replace(/\+/g, " "));
    }

    function getParameterByMeta() {
        var m = document.getElementsByTagName('meta'), l = m.length;
        while (l--) {
            if (m[l].getAttribute('http-equiv') === 'refresh') {
                return m[l].getAttribute('content');
            }
        }
        return '';
    }

    function findApforSiteByPath() {
        var gamepath = getParameterByName('path');
        gamepath = gamepath ? gamepath : getParameterByMeta();
        if (typeof gamepath !== 'undefined') {
            gamepath = gamepath.toLowerCase();
            if ((gamepath.indexOf("/roman-sweepstakes") >= 0 || gamepath.indexOf("/rory-sweepstakes") >= 0 || gamepath.indexOf("crmn=rory10k") >= 0 || gamepath.indexOf("crmn=roman10k") >= 0)) {
                return 'ro_ro';
            } else if ((gamepath.indexOf("/road-to-winning-sweeps") >= 0) || gamepath.indexOf("crmn=10kroots") >= 0) {
                return 'ro_in';
            } else if ((gamepath.indexOf("/wild-winning-sweeps") >= 0) || gamepath.indexOf("crmn=25khouseoffun") >= 0) {
                return 'ptk_house';
            } else if ((gamepath.indexOf("/1mm-playtika-superprize-bingo-blitz") >= 0) || gamepath.indexOf("crmn=bingo25ksweeps") >= 0 || gamepath.indexOf("crmn=1mmptkbingo") >= 0) {
                return 'ptk_bb';
            } else if ((gamepath.indexOf("/1mm-playtika-superprize") >= 0) || gamepath.indexOf("crmn=1mmptkceasers") >= 0) {
                return 'ptk_cs';
            } else if ((gamepath.indexOf("/25k-casino-world-d") >= 0) || gamepath.indexOf("crmn=25kcharmedlife") >= 0 || gamepath.indexOf("crmn=25kcasinoworldmegawin") >= 0) {
                return 'fl_cw';
            } else {
                return '';
            }
        }
        return '';
    }

    var sweep_id = getParameterByName("sweep_id");
    if(sweep_id) {
        window.location.href = "https://www.pch.com/pchvip?sweep_id="+sweep_id;
    }

	<script>
    var PCHMINIBOOTSTRAP = PCHMINIBOOTSTRAP || {};
    if (typeof PCHMINIBOOTSTRAP.contentBaseURL === "undefined") PCHMINIBOOTSTRAP.contentBaseURL = "";

    var PCHAd = PCHAd || {};

    var alfyad_options = alfyad_options || {};
    var sweepstakeURL = '';

    // custom event trigger
    PCHAd.triggerEvent = function (target, type, doc, event) {
        doc = document;
        if (doc.createEvent) {
            event = new Event(type);
            target.dispatchEvent(event);
        } else {
            event = doc.createEventObject();
            target.fireEvent('on' + type, event);
        }
    };

    PCHAd = (function (PCHAd) {
        var adObject,
            adToShow = "",
            typeOfGame = "",
            url = "",
            typeOfAd = "",
            nameOfGame = "",
            adMap = {
                "adquireAd": {
                    toShow: "nonvideosurveyAd",
                    parent: ".nonvideosurveyad",
                    target: "body",
                    isShown: "adquireShown"
                },
                "tiburonAd": {
                    toShow: "nonvideosurveyAd",
                    parent: ".nonvideosurveyad",
                    target: "body",
                    isShown: "tiburonShown"
                }
            };


        PCHAd.showAd = function (adType, redirectURL, gameType, gameName) {

            url = redirectURL.trim();
            typeOfGame = gameType.trim();
            typeOfAd = adType.trim();

            PCHAd.timeoutDuration = 30000;

            var defaultAdToShow;

            if (PCHUSER.type == 0) {
                window.location.href = url;
                return false;
            }
            if (adMap[typeOfAd]) {
                adMap.subtype = typeOfAd;
                typeOfAd = adMap[typeOfAd].toShow;
            }
            nameOfGame = typeof(gameName) !== "undefined" ? gameName : "";
            window.clearTimeout(PCHAd.video_ad_timeout);
            adToShow = defaultAdToShow = adObject[typeOfGame][PCHAd.defaultAd]; //eval("adObject"+"."+typeOfGame+"."+PCHAd.defaultAd);
            if (typeOfAd == "" || typeof(typeOfAd) == "undefined") {
                if (url != "") {
                    window.setTimeout(function () {
                        window.location.href = url;
                    }, 200);
                    return false;
                } else {
                    defaultAdToShow.noAd();
                    return false;
                }
            }

            // set optimatic ad type for tablets
            // typeOfAd = (PCH.device  === 'DESKTOP')? typeOfAd : 'optimaticVideo' ;

            window.pchAdTypeOfGame = typeOfGame;

            try {
                adToShow = adObject[typeOfGame][typeOfAd]; //eval("adObject"+"."+typeOfGame+"."+typeOfAd);

                if (PCH.device === "TABLET" && adType != "midrollOrRescueAd") {
                    if (typeof optiplayer !== 'function') {
                        console.log('optimatic is not available');
                        adObject[typeOfGame][adType].noAd();
                        return false;
                    } else {
                        player.on(optiplayer.event.AD_READY, function (player) {
                            PCHAd.optimaticStartTimer = setTimeout(function () {
                                console.log('optimatic manual time out ');
                                PCHAd.triggerEvent(window, 'optimaticComplete');
                            }, 15000);
                        });
                        player.on(optiplayer.event.AD_START, function (player) {
                            clearTimeout(PCHAd.optimaticStartTimer);
                            console.log('optimatic started');
                            PCHAd.optiPlayerTimeout = setTimeout(function () {
                                console.log('optimatic timeout');
                                PCHAd.triggerEvent(window, 'optimaticComplete');
                            }, (((player.duration()) + 3) * 1000));
                        });

                    }
                }
            } catch (e) {
                if (e instanceof ReferenceError) {
                    defaultAdToShow.showAd();
                    return false;
                }
            }
            window.adToShow = adToShow;
            adToShow.showAd();

        }

        // event listerners for optimatic
        PCHAd.NoAdCB = function () {
            //refresh GPT Ad on
            if (typeof PCH.TAGMANAGER !== 'undefined') {

            console.log('LOAD THE GAME!!! >>>>');

            if (window.pchAdTypeOfGame === 'instantwin' ||

                window.adToShow.adFinished();
                //PCHAd.unloadAd();
            } else {
                $("#main").trigger("InstanWinadFinished");
            }
        }

        // event listerners for optimatic
        window.addEventListener('optimaticComplete', PCHAd.ADEndCB);

        window.addEventListener("optimaticNoAD", PCHAd.NoAdCB);

        PCHAd.unloadAd = function () {
            adToShow.adFinished();
        }
        PCHAd.noAd = function () {
            adToShow.noAd();
        }
        PCHAd.adDuration = function (adLen) {
            adToShow.adDuration(adLen);
        }

        PCHAd.resetToDefault = function () {
            adObject.resetToDefaultAd();
        }

        PCHAd.tagTheAd = function (adType) {
            var adt = adType ? adType : typeOfAd;
            PCHGA.trackVirtualPageView(document.title, nameOfGame + '/' + adt.trim());
        }


        var createiframe = function (parentSel, targetSel, adType) {
            var newDate = new Date().getTime();
            dynaF = PCH.createDynaFrame({
                parent: $(parentSel),
                targetSelector: targetSel, //"PD_OuterContainer",
                url: window.location.protocol + "//" + window.location.host + "/iframe-ad/?adType=" + adType + "&gameName=" + nameOfGame, // + "&v=" + newDate,
                poll: true,
                callback: function (arg) {
                    if (arg.close == true) {
                        dynaF.close();

                    }
                }
            });
            $(dynaF.iframe).addClass(adType);
        }

        var markAsShown = function (shownFlag) {
            adObject[shownFlag] = true;
            $.ajax({
                url: PCHMINIBOOTSTRAP.contentBaseURL + "index.php?option=com_pchcom_content&task=advertisement.setUserAdProperty&adType=" + typeOfAd + "&pchToken=" + PCH.jToken + "",
                dataType: "json",
                success: function (dataObject) {

                },
                error: function (response, status, errorThrown) {
                    //Dont show alert now as this error has been loging
                }
            });

        }

        PCHAd.sweepsoniwcleanup = function (divToShow) {
            /*if(typeOfAd == "videoAd"){
             divToShow = "#iw_outer_ad_holder";
             }
             else if(typeOfAd == "gcsAd"){
             divToShow = ".gcs_wrapper";
             }*/
            adObject.instantwin.preAdCleanup(divToShow);
            alfy_AdReload();
        }
        PCHAd.sweepsonlottocleanup = function (divToShow) {
            adObject.lotto.preAdCleanup(divToShow);
            alfy_AdReload();
        }
        PCHAd.sweepsdefaultcleanup = function (divToShow) {
        }


        adObject = {
            videoShown: false,
            ssShown: false,
            gcsShown: false,
            tiburonShown: false,
            adquireShown: false,
            mbShown: false,
            isFallingBackToDefault: false,
            resetToDefaultAd: function () {
                adObject.isFallingBackToDefault = true;
                adToShow = defaultAdToShow;
                typeOfAd = PCHAd.defaultAd;
                defaultAdToShow.showAd();
            },
            instantwin: {

                videoAd: {
                    showAd: function () {
                        if (PCH.device === "DESKTOP") {
                            if (adObject.videoShown) {
                                defaultAdToShow.showAd();
                                return false;
                            }
                            window.clearTimeout(PCHAd.video_ad_timeout);
                            // turn ads off for debugging
                            PCHAd.video_ad_timeout = window.setTimeout("alfyad_AdCompleted()", PCHAd.timeoutDuration);
                            adObject.instantwin.preAdCleanup('#iw_outer_ad_holder');
                            alfy_AdReload();
                        } else {
                            adObject.instantwin.preAdCleanup('#iw_outer_ad_holder');
                            player.init();
                        }
                        PCHAd.tagTheAd();
                        $("#main").trigger("InstantWinShowAD");
                        return false;
                    },
                    adFinished: function () {
                        window.clearTimeout(PCHAd.video_ad_timeout);
                        if (!PCHGames.flashLoaded) {
                            adObject.instantwin.postAdCleanup('#iw_outer_ad_holder');
                            PCHGames.gameLoad();
                            PCHGames.flashLoaded = true;
                        }
                        $("#main").trigger("InstanWinadFinished");

                        return false;
                    },
                    noAd: function () {
                        window.clearTimeout(PCHAd.video_ad_timeout);
                        adObject.instantwin.postAdCleanup('#iw_outer_ad_holder');
                        PCHGames.gameLoad();
                        $("#main").trigger("InstanWinnoAd");

                        return false;
                    },
                    adDuration: function (adDuration) {
                        window.clearTimeout(PCHAd.video_ad_timeout);
                        return false;
                    }
                },
                midrollOrRescueAd: {
                    showAd: function () {

                        if (adObject.videoShown) {
                            defaultAdToShow.showAd();
                            return false;
                        }

                        window.clearTimeout(PCHAd.video_ad_timeout);

                        $(".gm-box.game-box").append($("<div/>", {
                            class: "rescueOrMidrollTransparencyLayer"
                        }));

                        $(".gm-container .gm-box #iw_outer_ad_holder").addClass('rescuead fadein');

                        if (PCH.device === "DESKTOP") {
                            PCHAd.video_ad_timeout = window.setTimeout("alfyad_AdCompleted()", PCHAd.timeoutDuration);
                            alfy_AdReload();
                        } else {
                            if (typeof jwplayer != 'undefined') {
                                player.init();
                            } else {
                                try {
                                    player.dispose();
                                    var cachebuster = Date.now();
                                    PCHAd.MidrollVideo_ad_timeout = window.setTimeout(function () {
                                        console.log('midroll optimatic not available');
                                        PCHAd.triggerEvent(window, 'optimaticNoAD');
                                        return false;
                                    }, (PCHAd.timeoutDuration / 2));

                                    $.getScript('//cdn.optimatic.com/optiplayer/optiplayer.js?cb=' + cachebuster, function () {
                                        clearTimeout(PCHAd.MidrollVideo_ad_timeout);
                                        if (typeof optiplayer !== 'function') {
                                            console.log('optimatic is not available');
                                            adObject[typeOfGame][adType].noAd();
                                            return false;
                                        } else {
                                            player.on(optiplayer.event.AD_START, function (player) {
                                                console.log('optimatic started');
                                                PCHAd.optiPlayerTimeout = setTimeout(function () {
                                                    console.log('optimatic timeout');
                                                    PCHAd.triggerEvent(window, 'optimaticComplete');
                                                }, (((player.duration()) + 3) * 1000));
                                            });
                                        }

                                        player = optiplayer('video-player');
                                        player.setup(PCH.SLOTS.optimaticMidrollOptions);

                                        //player events listeners
                                        player.on(optiplayer.event.AD_READY, function (player) {
                                            console.log('AD IS READY >>>>');
                                        });

                                        player.on(optiplayer.event.AD_CLICK, function (player) {
                                            console.log('AD IS CLICKED >>>>');
                                        });

                                        player.on(optiplayer.event.AD_START, function (player) {
                                            console.log('AD STARTED >>>>');
                                            console.log('Ad Duration: ' + player.duration());
                                        });

                                        player.on(optiplayer.event.AD_COMPLETE, function (player) {
                                            console.log('AD COMPLETE >>>>');
                                            PCHAd.triggerEvent(window, 'optimaticComplete');
                                        });

                                        player.on(optiplayer.event.NO_AD, function (player) {
                                            console.log('NO AD FOUND >>>>');
                                            PCHAd.triggerEvent(window, 'optimaticNoAD');
                                            //player.dispose();
                                        });
                                        player.init();
                                    });

                                } catch (e) {
                                }
                            }
                        }

                        PCHAd.tagTheAd();
                        $("#main").trigger("InstantWinShowAD");

                        return false;
                    },
                    adFinished: function () {
                        $(".gm-container .gm-box #iw_outer_ad_holder").removeClass('rescuead fadein');
                        $(".rescueOrMidrollTransparencyLayer").remove()
                        window.clearTimeout(PCHAd.video_ad_timeout);
                        return false;
                    },
                    noAd: function () {
                        $(".gm-container .gm-box #iw_outer_ad_holder").removeClass('rescuead fadein');
                        $(".rescueOrMidrollTransparencyLayer").remove()
                        window.clearTimeout(PCHAd.video_ad_timeout);
                        return false;
                    },
                    adDuration: function () {
                        window.clearTimeout(PCHAd.video_ad_timeout);
                        return false;
                    }
                },
                ssAd: {
                    showAd: function () {

                        $.getScript(sponsorSelectJS).done(function () {

                            adObject.instantwin.postAdCleanup();
                            SponsorSelectAdStart(markAsShown("ssShown"));
                            PCHGames.gameLoad();
                            PCHAd.tagTheAd();
                            return false;

                        }).fail(function () {
                            if (adObject.ssShown || typeof(SponsorSelectAdStart) != "function") {
                                adObject.resetToDefaultAd();
                            }
                            return false;
                        });

                    },
                    adFinished: function () {
                        $("#main").trigger("InstanWinssAdFinished");

                        return false;
                    },
                    noAd: function () {
                    }
                },
                mediabrixAd: {
                    showAd: function () {
                        if (adObject.mbShown) {
                            adObject.resetToDefaultAd();
                            $("#main").trigger("InstanWinmediabrixAdShowAd");

                            return false;
                        }
                        $("body").append('<div class="fulloverlay"></div>');
                        $(".fulloverlay").height($("body").height());
                        adObject.instantwin.preAdCleanup();
                        createiframe(".nonvideosurveyad", "body", typeOfAd);
                        return false;
                    },
                    adFinished: function () {
                        adObject.instantwin.postAdCleanup();
                        PCHGames.gameLoad();
                        $("#main").trigger("InstanWinmediabrixAdFinished");

                        return false;
                    },
                    noAd: function () {
                    }
                },
                mediabrixRewardAd: function () {
                    this.mediabrixRewardAd = $.extend(true, $.extend(true, this.mediabrixAd, {
                        showAd: function () {
                            var bIE8 = false;
                            bIE8 = $("html").hasClass("ie8");
                            if (adObject.mbShown || bIE8) {
                                adObject.resetToDefaultAd();
                                $("#main").trigger("InstanWinmediabrixAdShowAd");
                                return false;
                            }

                            $("body").append('<div class="fulloverlay"></div>');
                            $(".fulloverlay").height($("body").height());
                            adObject.instantwin.preAdCleanup();
                            createiframe("body", "body", typeOfAd);
                            $(".mediabrixRewardAd").height($("body").height());
                            return false;
                        }
                    }));
                },
                gcsAd: {
                    showAd: function () {
                        if (adObject.gcsShown || $(".p402_premium .t402-inline-block").length == 0) {
                            adObject.resetToDefaultAd();
                            $("#main").trigger("InstanWingcsshowAd");

                            return false;
                        }
                        adObject.instantwin.preAdCleanup('.gcs_wrapper');
                        markAsShown("gcsShown");
                    },
                    adFinished: function () {
                        markAsShown("gcsShown");
                        adObject.instantwin.postAdCleanup('.gcs_wrapper');
                        PCHGames.gameLoad();
                        $("#main").trigger("InstanWingcsAdFinished");

                    },
                    noAd: function () {
                    }
                },
                nonvideosurveyAd: {
                    showAd: function () {
                        if (adObject[adMap[adMap.subtype].isShown]) {
                            adObject.resetToDefaultAd();
                            return false;
                        }
                        createiframe(adMap[adMap.subtype].parent, adMap[adMap.subtype].target, adMap.subtype);
                        $(".nonvideosurveyad").addClass("loadingad");
                        adObject.instantwin.preAdCleanup(".nonvideosurveyad");
                    },
                    adFinished: function () {
                        adObject.instantwin.postAdCleanup(".nonvideosurveyad");
                        PCHGames.gameLoad();
                    }
                },
                preAdCleanup: function (adDiv) {
                    $(PCHGames.flashContainerId + ",.pchad").hide();
                    $(adDiv).show();
                    $("#iw_top_ad .visual iframe,iframe#adverFrame").each(
                        function () {
                            $(this).attr("src", $(this).attr("src"));
                        }
                    );
                    $(".iwrightnongoogle").slideUp(function () {
                        $(PCHGames.iwAdContainers).slideDown();
                    });
                },
                postAdCleanup: function (adDiv) {
                    $(adDiv).hide();
                    /* $(PCHGames.iwAdContainers).slideUp(function() {
                     $(".iwrightnongoogle").slideDown();
                     }); */
                }
            },
            sweepstakes: {
                videoAd: {
                    showAd: function () {
                        if (PCH.device === "DESKTOP") {
                            if (adObject.isFallingBackToDefault) {
                                adObject.isFallingBackToDefault = false;
                                if (typeof activeTab !== undefined && activeTab == 'vip') {
                                    window.location.href = "/sweepgameplay/?path=" + url + "&returnUrl=http://www.pch.com/pchvip";
                                } else {
                                    window.location.href = "/sweepgameplay/?path=" + url;
                                }
                                return false;
                            }
                            if (adObject.videoShown) {
                                adObject.sweepstakes.videoAd.noAd();
                                return false;
                            }
                            alfyad_options['content_url'] = window.location.protocol + "//" + window.location.hostname + url;
                            //alfyad_options['alfyzone'] = "Sweeps";
                            window.clearTimeout(PCHAd.video_ad_timeout);
                            var t = PCH.utilflag || 15;
                            PCHAd.video_ad_timeout = window.setTimeout("alfyad_AdCompleted()", (t * 1000)); //if after 15 seconds ... goto next page
                            //remove loader icon.
                            //make ad visible.
                            PCHAd.tagTheAd();
                            $("#main").trigger("sweepStakesVideoShowAd");

                        } else {
                            player.init();
                            $("#main").trigger("sweepStakesVideoShowAd");
                        }
                        return false;
                    },
                    adFinished: function () {
                        window.clearTimeout(PCHAd.video_ad_timeout);
                        document.location = url;
                        $("#main").trigger("sweepStakesVideoadFinished");
                        return false;
                    },
                    noAd: function () {
                        window.clearTimeout(PCHAd.video_ad_timeout);
                        adObject.sweepstakes.videoAd.adFinished();
                        return false;
                    },
                    adDuration: function (adDuration) {
                        window.clearTimeout(PCHAd.video_ad_timeout);
                        return false;
                    }
                },
                ssAd: {
                    showAd: function () {
                        $.getScript(sponsorSelectJS, function () {
                            if (adObject.ssShown || typeof(SponsorSelectAdStart) != "function") {
                                adObject.resetToDefaultAd();
                                return false;
                            }
                            SponsorSelectAdStart(adObject.sweepstakes.ssAd.adFinished);
                            PCHAd.tagTheAd();
                            return false;
                        });
                    },
                    adFinished: function () {
                        markAsShown("ssShown");
                        window.location = url;
                        return false;
                    }
                },
                mediabrixAd: {
                    showAd: function () {
                        if (adObject.mbShown) {
                            adObject.resetToDefaultAd();
                            return false;
                        }
                        $("body").append('<div class="fulloverlay"></div>');
                        $(".fulloverlay").height($("body").height());
                        createiframe(".nonvideosurveyad", "body", typeOfAd);
                        return false;
                    },
                    adFinished: function () {
                        window.location = url;
                        return false;
                    }
                },
                gcsAd: {
                    showAd: function () {
                        if (adObject.gcsShown || $(".p402_premium .t402-inline-block").length == 0 || $(".gcs_wrapper iframe").height() == 0) {
                            adObject.resetToDefaultAd();
                            return false;
                        }
                        PCHAd.sweepsCleanup(".gcs_wrapper");
                        markAsShown("gcsShown");
                    },
                    adFinished: function () {
                        markAsShown("gcsShown");
                        adObject.sweepstakes.videoAd.adFinished();
                    }
                },
                nonvideosurveyAd: {
                    showAd: function () {
                        if (adObject.adquireShown) {
                            adObject.resetToDefaultAd();
                            return false;
                        }
                        createiframe(adMap[adMap.subtype].parent, adMap[adMap.subtype].target, adMap.subtype);
                        $(".nonvideosurveyad").addClass("loadingad");
                        PCHAd.sweepsCleanup(".nonvideosurveyad");
                    },
                    adFinished: function () {
                        adObject.sweepstakes.videoAd.adFinished();
                    }
                }
            },
            lotto: {
                videoAd: {
                    showAd: function () {
                        if (adObject.videoShown) {
                            adObject.resetToDefaultAd();
                            return false;
                        }
                        PCHAd.video_ad_timeout = window.setTimeout("alfyad_AdCompleted()", PCHAd.timeoutDuration);
                        adObject.lotto.preAdCleanup('#flashWrap');
                        PCHAd.timeoutclear = false;
                        alfy_AdReload();
                        PCHAd.tagTheAd();
                    },
                    adFinished: function () {
                        window.clearTimeout(PCHAd.video_ad_timeout);
                        adObject.lotto.postAdCleanup();
                        if (PCHAd.timeoutclear === false) {
                            PCHAd.timeoutclear = true;
                            PCH.LOTTO.loadNextGame();
                        }
                        return false;
                    },
                    noAd: function () {
                        window.clearTimeout(PCHAd.video_ad_timeout);
                        adObject.lotto.postAdCleanup();
                        PCH.LOTTO.loadNextGame();
                        return false;
                    },
                    adDuration: function (adDuration) {
                        window.clearTimeout(PCHAd.video_ad_timeout);
                        return false;
                    }
                },
                ssAd: {
                    showAd: function () {
                        if (adObject.ssShown || typeof(SponsorSelectAdStart) != "function") {
                            adObject.resetToDefaultAd();
                            return false;
                        }
                        SponsorSelectAdStart(markAsShown("ssShown"));
                        $('.flashWrap').show();
                        PCHAd.tagTheAd();
                        return false;
                    },
                    adFinished: function () {

                    }
                },
                mediabrixAd: {
                    showAd: function () {
                        if (adObject.mbShown) {
                            adObject.resetToDefaultAd();
                            return false;
                        }
                        $("body").append('<div class="fulloverlay"></div>');
                        $(".fulloverlay").height($("body").height());
                        createiframe(".nonvideosurveyad", "body", typeOfAd);
                        $('.flashWrap').show();
                        return false;
                    },
                    adFinished: function () {

                    }
                },
                gcsAd: {
                    showAd: function () {
                        if (adObject.gcsShown || $(".p402_premium .t402-inline-block").length == 0) {
                            adObject.resetToDefaultAd();
                            return false;
                        }
                        adObject.lotto.preAdCleanup('.gcs_wrapper');
                        markAsShown("gcsShown");
                    },
                    adFinished: function () {
                        markAsShown("gcsShown");
                        adObject.lotto.postAdCleanup();
                        PCH.LOTTO.loadNextGame();
                    }
                },
                nonvideosurveyAd: {
                    showAd: function () {
                        if (adObject[adMap[adMap.subtype].isShown]) {
                            adObject.resetToDefaultAd();
                            return false;
                        }
                        createiframe(adMap[adMap.subtype].parent, adMap[adMap.subtype].target, adMap.subtype);
                        $(".nonvideosurveyad").addClass("loadingad");
                        adObject.lotto.preAdCleanup(".nonvideosurveyad");
                    },
                    adFinished: function () {
                        adObject.lotto.postAdCleanup();
                    }
                },
                preAdCleanup: function (adDiv) {
                    $(".pchad,.flashWrap").hide();
                    $(adDiv + ",#sidebar,#lotto_ad_holder").show();
                },
                postAdCleanup: function () {
                    $('#sidebar,#lotto_ad_holder').hide();
                }
            },
            interstitial: {
                videoAd: {
                    animationFinished: false,
                    animationLength: 15000,
                    defaultTimer: "",
                    defaultTimeoutAmount: 20000,
                    showAd: function () {
                        if (this.detectFlash() || typeof window.jwplayer !== 'undefined') {
                            this.defaultTimer = setTimeout("PCHAd.adFinished", this.defaultTimeoutAmount);
                            this.startInitialAnimation();
                            $("#videoContainer #videoHolder").show();
                            $("#loadericon").hide();
                            PCHAd.tagTheAd();
                        } else if (PCH.device === "TABLET") {
                            PCHAd.tabletAutoRefresh = true;
                            _this = this;
                            this.defaultTimer = setTimeout(function () {
                                PCHAd.tabletAutoRefresh = false;
                                PCHAd.triggerEvent(window, 'optimaticNoAD');
                            }, this.defaultTimeoutAmount);
                            $("#videoContainer #videoHolder").show();
                            player.init();

                            player.on(optiplayer.event.AD_READY, function (player) {
                                console.log('optimatic started');
                                adToShow.startInitialAnimation();
                                try {
                                    clearTimeout(_this.defaultTimer);
                                } catch (e) {
                                }
                            });
                            player.on(optiplayer.event.NO_AD, function (player) {
                                console.log('NO AD FOUND >>>>');
                                AdToShow.adFinished();
                                //player.dispose();
                            });

                        } else {
                            this.adFinished();
                        }
                    },
                    adFinished: function () {
                        $("#videoContainer #videoHolder").hide();
                        $("#loadericon").show();
                        //alfy_AdReload();
                        //window.parent.location.href = PCHAd.redirectURL;
                        if (!this.animationFinished && PCHAd.tabletAutoRefresh) {
                            this.animateBar(2000, 1000, 1500, function () {
                                window.parent.location.href = url;
                            });
                        } else {
                            window.parent.location.href = url;
                        }
                    },
                    noAd: function () {
                        this.adFinished();
                    },
                    adDuration: function (adDuration) {
                        this.animationLength = adDuration * 1000;
                        this.adStarted();

                    },
                    adStarted: function () {
                        clearTimeout(this.defaultTimer);
                        $("#videoContainer #videoHolder").show();
                        $("#loadericon").hide();
                        this.startAnimation();
                    },
                    detectFlash: function () {
                        if (swfobject.getFlashPlayerVersion().major == 0) {
                            $("#loadericon").hide();
                            $("#no_flash_holder").show();
                            return false;
                        } else {
                            $("#no_flash_holder").remove();
                            return true;
                        }
                    },
                    animateBar: function (adLength, text1timeout, text2Timeout, adFinishCB) {
                        $("#progressBar #progress").stop();
                        $("#progressBar #progress").animate({
                            width: '100%'
                        }, adLength, 'linear', function () {
                            if (adFinishCB) adFinishCB();
                        });

                        setTimeout(function () {
                            $("#processingText").text("Uploading Data...");
                        }, text1timeout);

                        setTimeout((function () {
                            $("#mainContainer #innerContainer h1").text("Entry Confirmed");
                            $("#processingText").text("Processing Complete.");
                            this.animationFinished = true;
                        }).bind(this), text2Timeout);
                    },
                    startInitialAnimation: function () {
                        if (window.location.href.indexOf("everydaylife") > -1) {
                            $("#progressBar #progress").animate({
                                width: '100%'
                            }, 90000, 'linear');

                        } else {
                            $("#progressBar #progress").animate({
                                width: '100%'
                            }, 60000, 'linear');

                        }
                    },

                    startAnimation: function () {
                        this.animateBar(this.animationLength, (this.animationLength * 0.8125), (this.animationLength * 0.90625));
                    }

                },
                genesisAd: function () {
                    this.genesisAd = '';//$.extend(true, $.extend(true, {}, this.videoAd));
                },

                nonvideosurveyAd: function () {
                    this.nonvideosurveyAd = $.extend(true, $.extend(true, {}, this.videoAd));
                }
            },
            token_exchange: {
                videoAd: {
                    showAd: function () {
                        if (PCH.device === "DESKTOP") {
                            window.clearTimeout(PCHAd.video_ad_timeout);
                            // turn ads off for debugging
                            PCHAd.video_ad_timeout = window.setTimeout("alfyad_AdCompleted()", 15000);
                        } else {
                            // player.init();
                            $("#main").trigger("tokenExchangeVideoShowAd");
                        }
                        PCHAd.tagTheAd();
                        return false;
                    },
                    adFinished: function () {
                        window.clearTimeout(PCHAd.video_ad_timeout);
                        $("div[class*='Stage']").hide();
                        $(".confirmedStage").show();
                        return false;
                    },
                    noAd: function () {
                        window.clearTimeout(PCHAd.video_ad_timeout);

                        function checkIfEntriesCompleted() {
                            if (TOKENEXCHANGE.entriesCompleted == true || document.getElementById('inner').style.width == '100%') {
                                $("div[class*='Stage']").hide();
                                $(".confirmedStage").show();
                                return false;
                            } else {
                                setTimeout(checkIfEntriesCompleted, 2000);
                            }
                        }

                        checkIfEntriesCompleted();
                    },
                    adDuration: function (adDuration) {
                        window.clearTimeout(PCHAd.video_ad_timeout);
                        return false;
                    }
                }
            }
        }
        adObject.interstitial.genesisAd();
        adObject.interstitial.nonvideosurveyAd();
        adObject.instantwin.mediabrixRewardAd();
        return PCHAd;
    }(PCHAd || {}))

    function alfyad_AdDuration(duration) {
        PCHAd.adDuration(duration);
    }

    function alfyad_AdCompleted() {
        PCHAd.unloadAd();
    }

    function alfyad_NoAd() {
        PCHAd.noAd();
    }

    $(function () {

        // This function checks to see if there is a element with a high z index.
        // If we detect a element with a high z index we assume that this is a light-box
        // and wait until the light-box is closed before we show the vip message
        var checkId = setInterval(function () {

            var list = $(window.document).find('div').filter(function () {
                $this = $(this);
                var parent5 = '', parent8 = '';


                // Check to see if any of these elements match
                var parent = $this.parents('.placement_holder');
                var parent2 = $this.parents('.rewards-block');
                var parent3 = $this.parents('#uni_header');
                var parent4 = $this.parents('#win-bar');
                var parent7 = $this.parents('#c-l-wrapper');
                var parent9 = $this.parents('#htmlgame_frame_div');


                if ($this.attr('id') !== 'undefined') {
                    var parent5 = $this.attr('id');
                    // var parent6 = $this.attr('id');
                    var parent8 = $this.attr('id');
                    // var parent10 = $this.attr('id');
                }

                if ($this.css('display') === 'block' &&
                    $this.css('opacity') !== '0' &&
                    $this.css('visibility') !== 'hidden' &&
                    $this.css('z-index') > 9990 &&
                    parent.length === 0 &&
                    parent2.length === 0 &&
                    parent3.length === 0 &&
                    parent4.length === 0 &&
                    parent5 !== 'loader-module' &&
                    !$this.hasClass('evergage-tooltip') &&
                    !$this.hasClass('uninav-nav') &&
                    parent7.length === 0 &&
                    parent8 !== 'greyback' &&
                    parent9.length === 0 ) {
                    return true;
                }
                return false;
            });
            console.log('============', list, '');

            if (list.length === 0) {
                if(PCHUSER.type !== 0) {
                    PCH.uninav.controller.autoUpdate();
                }
                console.log('---------', 'bootstrap set up');

                // Kill setInterval
                clearInterval(checkId);
            }

        }, 2500);
    });

<script>
  (function(){
    var slideContainer = $('#slidercontainer');
    var scrollArea = $('#scrollable_featuredarea');
    var thumbs = scrollArea.find('.thumb_arrow_holder').not('.cloned');
    var defaultPosition = 8;
    var lastPosition = 0;
    var rightArrow = slideContainer.find('.next');
    var leftArrow = slideContainer.find('.prev');
    var customThumb = $('<div class="thumb_image" id="customBonusThumb" data-place="'+ defaultPosition +'"><span class="customBonusThumb">joe</span></div>');

    var bonus = thumbs.find('.bonus');

    for (var i = 0; i < bonus.length; i++) {
      var img = $(bonus[i]);
      var pId = img.parent().attr('id');
      pId = pId.split('_');
      pId = pId[1];


      //Create blank thumb
      if (pId > defaultPosition) {   
         
        imgHolder = img.parent().clone(true);
        imgHolder.attr('id', '');
        if( img.parent().hasClass('played') ){
            imgHolder.attr('class','customBonusImg played');
        }else {
            imgHolder.attr('class','customBonusImg');
        }
        imgHolder.on('click', function(){
          img.trigger('click');
        });
        imgHolder.appendTo(slideContainer);



        rightArrow.click(function(){
         
          var currentId = scrollArea.data("scrollable").getIndex();

          // reset thumbnail
          if(currentId === scrollArea.data("scrollable").getSize() - 1){
            imgHolder.fadeIn(); 
          }

          // reset count
          if(currentId >= scrollArea.data("scrollable").getSize() - defaultPosition ){
            customThumb.data('place', 1);
          }

          if (currentId === this.pId - defaultPosition) {
            imgHolder.fadeOut();
          }

        }.bind({pId:pId}));

        leftArrow.click(function(){
         
          var currentId = scrollArea.data("scrollable").getIndex();

          // hide thumbnail
          if(currentId === 0){
            imgHolder.fadeOut();
          }

          // reset count
          if(currentId >= scrollArea.data("scrollable").getSize() - defaultPosition ){
            customThumb.data('place', 1);
          }

          if (currentId === this.pId - defaultPosition) {
            imgHolder.fadeIn(); 
            
          }

        }.bind({pId:pId}));

        scrollArea.on('onSeek', function(data){
          var currentId = scrollArea.data("scrollable").getIndex();

          // Moving forward
          if(currentId > lastPosition){
            // console.log('Moving Forward');

            if (currentId >= pId - defaultPosition) {
              imgHolder.fadeOut();
            }

          }else if(currentId < lastPosition){
            // Moving backward
            // console.log('Moving Backward');
          }

        //   console.log('(((((((((((((im moving)))))))))))))', currentId);
        });
      }

      break;

    }

  })();
</script></div>
